<div class="review__content">
<div class="review__header">
<div class="review__rating-block">
<div class="review__rating">
<div aria-label="Rating is 5.0 out of 5 points" class="rating-stars rating-stars--1-size">

<div aria-hidden="true" class="rating-stars__star rating-stars__star--full">★</div>

<div class="review__review-source">Reviewed on G2</div>
</div>
</div>
<div aria-label="Text of review">
<div class="review__main-quote">"Real-Time SEO Monitoring/Auditing is the Future"</div>
<div class="review__full-review typo">
<p>Traditional crawlers crawl at a single point in time, ContentKing is great because I get real-time updates of potential SEO issues as they arise. Real-time alerts, combined with custom extraction is a game-changer for finding the root of technical issues for SEO.</p>
<p>I can combat site changes (that will negatively impact SEO) made by other teams. I can enable cross-functional teams with access to the alerting functions to help their processes.</p>
<p>Within the first week, I was able to find a technical issue on the site that our traditional crawler did not see (due to the timing of our traditional scheduled crawls).</p>
</div>
</div>
</div>
</div>

<div aria-label="Text of review">
<div class="review__main-quote">"I couldn't recommend ContentKing more"</div>
<div class="review__full-review typo">
<p>Hands down one of my all-time favorite tools. Wherever I go, (project to project, one job to the next) I take ContentKing with me :) Such a time saver and probably one of the best customer service teams out there. Always helpful, super fast to respond, and impressively knowledgeable. Thanks for your support!</p>
<p>Overall excellent product development. Timely alerts. The granularity of alert trigger setup. Consolidating relevant information in one place. Access for the whole team. Easy sharing of views.</p>

<div aria-label="Text of review">
<div class="review__main-quote">"ContentKing has helped us keep an eye on problematic site changes"</div>
<div class="review__full-review typo">
<p>ContentKing is amazingly accurate. I've used other site scanning tools, including the REALLY expensive ones, and ContentKing just does a better job and is a fraction of the price. ContentKing's team is also THE SWEETEST. We really value them as partners and we have a great relationship with them. They even took us out for beers at BrightonSEO. One of the most useful things about ContentKing is the page history feature. It's so helpful to be able to go back in time to see when an issue started. This helps us narrow down releases that could have had an impact. We LOVE ContentKing.</p>
<p>We are solving the problem of not being able to be everywhere at once. We run a MASSIVE site that is constantly changing. We simply cannot be everywhere. ContentKing helps us keep an eye on the content changes that could have a major SEO impact down the road.</p>
</div>

<div aria-label="Text of review">
<div class="review__main-quote">"Take your SEO and online performance serious, use ContentKing!"</div>
<div class="review__full-review typo">
<p>It instantly gives a complete overview of the status of your website. Instant action points and an indication of how well you are performing. Also, insert the website of your competitors, and you can benchmark immediately.</p>
<p>In addition, the specific elements such as the segments, combined data and issue monitor provide a good starting point for your strategy. What works well and what doesn't with a direct answer to the "why not" question.</p>
<p>Next to that, the monitoring is awesome, fully customizable to your needs. The bonus is the excellent chat function, the greatest support I have experienced in Tooling.</p>

<div class="review__full-review typo">

<p>Beyond monitoring, it's a very useful tool to find optimization opportunities.</p>
<p>ContentKing helps us make sure our site is displaying what we expect it to show to users and that we are made aware if anything deviates from that. It also helps us find new improvement ideas, filtering pages based on their type and relevance.</p>

<div class="review__main-quote">"Couldn't work without it!"</div>
<div class="review__full-review typo">
<p>ContentKing is great for when multiple teams are working across a website, which can often lead to unknown site changes going live. It's also great for when new changes result in bugs on-site and actions that require immediate attention. We're also able to monitor a high number of websites at a very top level, all in one place.</p>
<p>We're alerted promptly and efficiently when issues occur onsite; we've been able to solve a wide range of issues. For example, we can quickly fix missing H1s or accidental changes within the robots.txt or be alerted when primary revenue-driving pages on site have gone down unexpectedly.</p>

<div aria-label="Text of review">
<div class="review__main-quote">"Easy website monitoring across multiple domains"</div>
<div class="review__full-review typo">
<p>Our marketeers use ContentKing to safeguard the SEO quality of our landing pages. At the same time ContentKing provides instant monitoring of platform issues, which is very convenient to keep an eye on the impact of platform releases. Our company manages a portfolio of 42 websites, so a tool that can monitor easily across different domains is essential for us.</p>
<p>In companies where you work with multiple websites, regular output of new content, multiple teams/marketeers, ContentKing can help create order in the chaos.</p>

<div aria-label="Text of review">
<div class="review__main-quote">"Must-have software for serious SEOs, webmasters, businesses"</div>
<div class="review__full-review typo">
<p>Prior to ContentKing we had no overview of what was happening and changing on the sites we were responsible for. Even though we were proactive and able to get sites back on track when clients or other people with access changed something they shouldn't have, ContentKing makes this easier and has reduced the operational burden of doing it all manually with little to no help from software.</p>
<p>I can't imagine a day without ContentKing on our client sites anymore, and honestly can't believe that there are people running sites that don't use it quite yet. If you've ever felt like you're losing your hair keeping track of the sites you manage, just know that there is ContentKing here to make your life easier.</p>

<div aria-label="Text of review">
<div class="review__main-quote">"Real-time SEO monitoring of website super easy"</div>
<div class="review__full-review typo">
<p>The alert system is robust. It can alert you about any change that impacts your website in real-time.
Due to Core Web Vitals I am migrating my Word Press website from a page builder to Gutenberg blocks. There are a lot of changes I need to address, deleting some plugins and installing others for instance. These changes can break things from an SEO perspective, and ContentKing helps us monitor all aspects of our website in real-time and sends alerts just in time before we even realize that something is wrong. Moreover, without ContentKing, we could not be aware of this.</p>

<div class="review__main-quote">"You won't find anything that beats ContentKing"</div>
<div class="review__full-review typo">
<p>After looking for a website monitoring tool for about 3 months, we landed with ContentKing. Contentking is the only tool that monitors both SEO issues, redirect issues, broken links and much more.</p>

Making it a one stop tool for everything you need to know about your sites health, right in your browser without 3rd party tools. Its easy to understand and easy to configure, and if you don't, support is amazing!</p>
<p>If you are reading this review, stop and just sign up already, ContentKing is the King of monitoring tools.</p>

<div aria-label="Text of review">
<div class="review__main-quote">"A Tremendous Tool"</div>
<div class="review__full-review typo">
<p>Add a website to ContentKing and any changes made to that website that might affect it's SEO will be automatically tracked so that you can safely experiment with various elements and revert back to prior versions if required. No more manually tracking changes by hand in a spreadsheet, each time even the slightest change is made, ContentKing will pick it up and add it to a growing list of every change made to that page.</p>
<p>Overall, ContentKing is an indispensable tool for any SEO. The user interface is super clean and very easy to navigate, the tracking is very accurate and super reliable and I'm able to rest easy, knowing that I'll always have a reliable record of changes made to a page in the event that I need to restore previous versions. Thank you ContentKing!</p>
</div>

<div class="review__main-quote">"Keep your site optimized for peak website performance at ALL times"</div>
<div class="review__full-review typo">
<p>We are currently using ContentKing for real-time monitoring of our sites (medium size sites). It comes very handy when you don't want to spend time crawling your sites every week to detect any issues. With that tool, you will be aware of any changes your dev team made, as well as your content teams. If your dev team added a no-index tag by mistake, you will instantly be notified. <p>ContentKing is well suited if your are managing different blogs or ecommerce stores and you need to keep an eye on any changes made. Good pricing structure based on the number of pages you have. <div class="review__main-quote">"ContentKing team goes above and beyond in their customer service and support"</div>
<div class="review__full-review typo">
<p>The tool does a great job catching SEO-related issues quickly, and alerting us when one of our sites needs immediate attention.</p>
<p>ContentKing has allowed us to monitor a slew of websites for changes as we're not always privy to content additions/subtractions/changes before they're implemented.</p>
<p>Additionally, we leverage the tool as a quick content inventory that's always up-to-date and includes a change history, which has been great!</p>

<div aria-label="Text of review">
<div class="review__main-quote">"Want some good insights on your websites content? Trust the King."</div>
<div class="review__full-review typo">
<p>SEO Auditing has never been easier, with the King you get insightful and real-time data on how your websites are doing. It provides great insights into your pages and related SEO content, so you can monitor your overall website (and content) health. It's properly designed and really easy to use and configure.</p>
<p>ContentKing is great to help you adjust your website SEO content to make pages adhere to better standards, and thus relate to better SEO results overall. It also provides great insights into the technical working of your websites, like http status info and simple things like sitemap and robots.txt files. The tool also provides reasons as to why certain checks are the way there are, through the ContentKing Academy, so you might even learn some extra things along the way. And if a certain check is not something you want to follow up on, you can always let the app ignore certain issues.</p>
</div>
</div>
</div>

<div aria-label="Text of review">
<div class="review__main-quote">"A must-have for agencies"</div>
<div class="review__full-review typo">
<p>If you're looking for a advanced monitoring system (among other features but this one is the most prominent) that's easy to implement (click of a button) which requires nothing other than the domain name you should definitely look up ContentKing.</p>
<p>What I like the most about ContentKing is the alerts system. Unlike tools like Uptimerobot (or similar ones) you get more than just "Website is down". You get a detailed explanation of important changes whether the website is down, canonicals gets changed, headers changed etc. With ContentKing we're able to be proactive towards our clients rather than reactive.</p>
<p>As an agency we deal with a lot of clients, being able to stay up-to-date on the changes their making without spending a lot of time every week on looking it up is immensely helpful. Because of this we're also able to be proactive towards our clients when major issues arise instead of noticing it weeks later.</p>
</div>
</div>
</div>

<div class="review__content">

<div class="review__rating-block">
<div class="review__rating">
<div aria-label="Rating is 5.0 out of 5 points" class="rating-stars rating-stars--1-size">

<div class="review__review-source">Reviewed on G2</div>

<div aria-label="Text of review">
<div class="review__main-quote">"Superb software, superb customer service!"</div>
<div class="review__full-review typo">
<p>ContentKing is fantastic for monitoring website stability and onpage changes. If you have "a lot of cooks in the kitchen" working on your website, it's a must-have in order to ensure that you don't get any nasty surprises in your SEO from someone changing something they shouldn't have.</p>
<p>I successfully used ContentKing to diagnose a Kubernetes architecture issue with one client. Pages from a lower environment (including the meta robots noindex) were being intermittently shown in production, and ContentKing was able to provide us the data to show that "hey, you're noindexing your website for about 5 minutes at a time, intermittently, throughout the day." It, of course, saved the client's SEO and it went a long way with maintaining our relationship with them.</p>
<p>Lastly, CK's customer service is great. Everyone is fantastic and responsive, and they will go out of their way to help you solve a problem.</p>
</div>
</div>

<div aria-label="Text of review">
<div class="review__main-quote">"ContentKing delivers"</div>
<div class="review__full-review typo">
<p>Unlike other crawlers, ContentKing is constantly scouring my websites, letting me know when there are issues that I may not have otherwise caught for a while. It's an invaluable tool for any SEO with large sites.</p>
<p>ContentKing allows us to resolve SEO related issues post-release. We've been able to catch certain issues before they've been live for too long. It also gives us peace of mind.</p>
<p>I don't really have a dislike for the tool. It "does what it says on the tin".</p>

<div class="review__main-quote">"ContentKing is a must for all SEOs"</div>
<div class="review__full-review typo">
<p>The main thing I love about ContentKing is that I feel like we are on top of any potential issues when monitoring a website. The ease of seeing content in tags, links, and relationships of pages is just fantastic.</p>
<p>If you need to monitor multiple websites and most importantly changes to websites that can negatively affect rankings then ContentKing is awesome. If a developer suddenly changes pages / menu / links on a website it can massively effect rankings – I no longer have this worry.</p>

<div class="review__header">
<div class="review__rating-block">
<div class="review__rating">
<div aria-label="Rating is 5.0 out of 5 points" class="rating-stars rating-stars--1-size">
<div aria-hidden="true" class="rating-stars__star rating-stars__star--full">★</div>
<div aria-hidden="true" class="rating-stars__star rating-stars__star--full">★</div>
<div aria-hidden="true" class="rating-stars__star rating-stars__star--full">★</div>
<div aria-hidden="true" class="rating-stars__star rating-stars__star--full">★</div>
<div aria-hidden="true" class="rating-stars__star rating-stars__star--full">★</div>
</div>
</div>
<div class="review__review-source">Reviewed on Capterra</div>
</div>
</div>
<div aria-label="Text of review">
<div class="review__main-quote">"It was great! Steven always answered questions promptly."</div>
<div class="review__full-review typo">
<p>Having live updates is key here – often time SEO teams will only be crawling their sites once per month with tools like screaming frog (which is fine I guess) but where ContentKing really smashes it out of the park is with live updates. It automatically tells if something has gone wrong, and if you’re doing crawls only on the last day of the month, you may not have noticed for weeks!</p>
</div>
</div>
</div>

<div aria-label="Role of author" class="review__job-title">

<div class="review__content">
<div class="review__header">
<div class="review__rating-block">
<div class="review__rating">
<div aria-label="Rating is 5.0 out of 5 points" class="rating-stars rating-stars--1-size">
<div aria-hidden="true" class="rating-stars__star rating-stars__star--full">★</div>
<div aria-hidden="true" class="rating-stars__star rating-stars__star--full">★</div>
<div aria-hidden="true" class="rating-stars__star rating-stars__star--full">★</div>
<div aria-hidden="true" class="rating-stars__star rating-stars__star--full">★</div>
<div aria-hidden="true" class="rating-stars__star rating-stars__star--full">★</div>
</div>
</div>
<div class="review__review-source">Reviewed on Capterra</div>
</div>
</div>
<div aria-label="Text of review">
<div class="review__main-quote">"Content King gives a very clear insight of what's going on on my website at any time !"</div>
<div class="review__full-review typo">
<p>Its reports are very complete and you can customize them to better fit your needs by ignoring some issues (which are not truly important). Also, every time I had the slightest issue and I had contacted the customer support, there were very patient and nice to help me understand what was going on or how could I achieve what I wanted to do.
From a UX point of view, the interface is very user-friendly and nice to use. You have a general overview of your website’s situation and then you can dig deeper into what matters to you.
What I also like is that they keep a history of what has happened on the pages so that you can go back in time and assess the improvements made on a specific page or understand when and why a page started to derail.</p>
</div>
</div>
</div>

				Web Designer
			</div>
<div aria-label="Company" class="review__company">Zellous Design</div>
</div>
<div aria-label="The publication date" class="review__date">
			April 2018
		</div>
</div>
<div class="review__content">
<div class="review__header">
<div class="review__rating-block">
<div class="review__rating">
<div aria-label="Rating is 5.0 out of 5 points" class="rating-stars rating-stars--1-size">
<div aria-hidden="true" class="rating-stars__star rating-stars__star--full">★</div>
<div aria-hidden="true" class="rating-stars__star rating-stars__star--full">★</div>
<div aria-hidden="true" class="rating-stars__star rating-stars__star--full">★</div>
<div aria-hidden="true" class="rating-stars__star rating-stars__star--full">★</div>
<div aria-hidden="true" class="rating-stars__star rating-stars__star--full">★</div>
</div>
</div>
<div class="review__review-source">Reviewed on Capterra</div>
</div>
</div>
<div aria-label="Text of review">
<div class="review__main-quote">"Website SEO (and general health) monitoring made easy"</div>
<div class="review__full-review typo">
<p>1) Website Overview: With Content King I can see the whole picture of a website: How the URLs are laid out, the health score of each page, and any problems/issues they may have (including broken links or pages that can’t be indexed).</p>
<p>2) Track Changes: What truly sets Content King apart from any other scanning tool I’ve used is: Content King tracks changes. It’s not a one-off scan, or merely a recurring scan. Content King keeps a running list of the changes for each page. If you’re in the businesses of monitoring client websites and providing maintenance, this is a game changer.</p>
<p>Example: Content King notified me that several pages had gone “”missing”” on one of my client’s sites. Turns out, they were consolidating several pages into one new page. However, they hadn’t setup any 301 redirects to let Google know they weren’t merely removed. Thanks to Content King, I was aware of the change and was able to advise my client accordingly.</p>
<p>3) Easy to Use: Content King has a wonderfully designed user interface. Feels fresh and new.</p>
<p>4) Website Migration: I haven’t had the opportunity to use Content King to monitor the success of a website migration yet, but I’m looking forward to that.</p>
<p>5) Notifications and Reports: Content King notifies me of any major issues that pop up on a website, and they also send a weekly summary/graph so I can see an overview of what’s going on with each of the websites I monitor.</p>
<p>6) Support: Very helpful and responsive support.</p>
</div>
</div>
</div>

<div class="review__content">
<div class="review__header">
<div class="review__rating-block">
<div class="review__rating">
<div aria-label="Rating is 5.0 out of 5 points" class="rating-stars rating-stars--1-size">
<div aria-hidden="true" class="rating-stars__star rating-stars__star--full">★</div>
<div aria-hidden="true" class="rating-stars__star rating-stars__star--full">★</div>
<div aria-hidden="true" class="rating-stars__star rating-stars__star--full">★</div>
<div aria-hidden="true" class="rating-stars__star rating-stars__star--full">★</div>
<div aria-hidden="true" class="rating-stars__star rating-stars__star--full">★</div>
</div>
</div>
<div class="review__review-source">Reviewed on Product Hunt</div>
</div>
</div>
<div aria-label="Text of review">
<div class="review__main-quote">"The most helpful hands-off SEO tool I've ever used"</div>
<div class="review__full-review typo">
<p>Onsite SEO has always been inherently problematic in that it's almost entirely reactive. You don't typically notice issues until they're already affecting your site. ContentKing tackles that issue, IMO, quite effectively: It monitors your site for changes in real time and alerts you as soon as anything bad happens.</p>
<p>Every SEO I know has experienced a situation where one small (usually inadvertent) change resulted in serious site issues. The accompanying panic and scramble to diagnose/fix aren't fun. And that's why I like ContentKing so much - it takes care of the little things so I don't have to, and frees up my time to focus on the bigger picture.</p>
</div>
</div>
</div>
</div>

<div aria-hidden="true" aria-labelledby="cookie-banner-policy-heading" aria-modal="true" class="dialog dialog--slide-in-effect" data-cookie-policy-version="f0cbb742597d5cb7e9db2f680777051bbd82001f" id="cookie-banner-policy" inert="" role="dialog">
<div class="cookie-consent-dlg">
<div class="cookie-consent-dlg__scrollable-container">
<div class="cookie-consent-dlg__content">
<div class="cookie-consent-dlg__heading">
<div class="cookie-consent-dlg__title" id="cookie-banner-policy-heading">Cookie Policy</div>
</div>
<div class="cookie-consent-dlg__text typo">
<p><em>Last updated January 24, 2022</em></p>
<p>When you use our website <a href="https://www.contentkingapp.com/">www.contentkingapp.com</a> (“Website”), we may place cookies. This Cookie Policy explains what cookies are and in which way cookies are stored on, and information is read from, your computer, mobile device and/or tablet (“Devices”). Please read this Cookie Policy carefully in order to understand what type of cookies ContentKing uses, the information we collect using cookies and how that information is used.</p>
<h2 id="what-are-cookies">What are cookies?</h2>
<p>Cookies are small text files which are stored on the browser or hard drive of your Device when you visit a webpage or use an application. Cookies may be needed to show the webpage or application on your Device and are also used to enhance the user experience. Cookies cannot damage your Devices or the files saved on it. There are different types of cookies. Some cookies come directly from our website (first party cookies) and others come from third parties which place cookies on our site (third party cookies).</p>
<p>Cookies can be stored for varying lengths of time on your browser or device. Session cookies are deleted from your computer or device when you close your web-browser. Persistent cookies will remain stored on your computer or Device until deleted or until they reach their expiry date.</p>
<h2 id="how-do-we-use-cookies">How do we use cookies?</h2>
<h3 id="essential-technical-cookies">Essential (Technical) cookies</h3>
<p>We try to provide an advanced and user-friendly website that adapts automatically to needs and wishes of our visitors and users. To achieve this, we use technical cookies to i.e. show you our Website, to make it function correctly, to create your ContentKing account, to sign you in and to manage your requests. These technical cookies are necessary for our website to function properly.</p>
<h3 id="functional-cookies">Functional cookies</h3>
<p>We also use functional cookies to remember your preferences and settings (as username, password, language etc.) and to help you to use the Website efficiently and effectively. These functional cookies are not strictly necessary for the functioning of our Website, but they add functionality for you and enhance your experience.</p>
<h3 id="analytical-cookies">Analytical cookies</h3>
<p>We use analytical cookies in order to collect statistics about the use and visits of the Website. These analytic cookies generate statistical and other information about website use by means of cookies, which are stored on users’ Devices. The information generated relating to our Website is used to create reports about the use of the Website. Analytical cookies may be placed without your consent, unless such cookies have an impact on your privacy. In such cases, prior consent will be asked for.</p>
<h3 id="google-analytics">Google Analytics</h3>
<p>We use Google Analytics cookies in order to collect statistics about the use and visits of the Website. With these analytical cookies a permanent cookie is saved on your device to register your use of the Website. Google Analytics analyses this data and provides us with the results. This way, we obtain insight into the traffic of the Website and the way in which the Website is used. Based on this information we are able to make specific adjustments to the Website.</p>
<p>The information that we obtain is transferred to Google and stored by Google on servers outside the European Economic Area. We have entered into a data processing agreement with Google in which agreements have been made regarding the processing of personal data.</p>
<p>If you would like more information about analytical cookies and their expiry date, please visit the Google Analytics <a href="https://developers.google.com/analytics/devguides/collection/gajs/cookie-usage">information page</a>. Google also offers an <a href="https://tools.google.com/dlpage/gaoptout?hl=en">opt-out option</a> for data collection within the scope of Google Analytics.</p>
<h3 id="marketing-cookies">Marketing cookies</h3>
<p>We use third party marketing cookies in order to follow your internet browsing behavior and collect data and information on your browsing behavior from various websites you visited. This information is used to make the content of the displayed advertisements as relevant as possible, and to limit repetition of the same advertisements.</p>
<h3 id="social-plug-ins">Social plug-ins</h3>
<p>By using the Website you can get access to social media websites, such as Facebook, Twitter and LinkedIn. These buttons come with a code which has been made by these networks themselves. Using these so called social plug-ins you can login to your social media profile and subsequently share information from the Website with others. With these social plug-ins third party marketing cookies are saved on your Devices. These cookies serve the purpose of optimizing your user experience.</p>
<p>Companies such as LinkedIn, Twitter and Facebook may share your personal data outside the European Economic Area. Please read our Privacy Policy <a href="/legal/privacy-policy/">here</a> and the respective social network’s privacy statement to see how these companies treat your (personal) data.</p>
<h3 id="pixels">Pixels</h3>
<p>We also place pixels of third parties. A pixel keeps track of your surfing behavior and how you use the Website. These data are aggregated and give us information about the target group that visits our website. Based on this information, we can show an advertisement to a specific or similar target group on the website of the third party that produced the pixel.</p>
<h2 id="disable-or-delete-cookies">Disable or delete cookies</h2>
<p>When you first visit the Website, we ask you to give consent for cookies that are not necessary or functional and that have an impact on your privacy. If you do not give consent, these cookies will not be placed. In that case, you may not be able to use all the functionalities on our Website.</p>
<p>You can configure your browser so that you do not receive any cookies the next time you use the website. You can read here how you can remove different types of cookies in different browsers. Please consult the help-function of your browser if your browser is not listed below.</p>
<ul>
<li><a href="https://support.google.com/chrome/answer/95647?co=GENIE.Platform%3DDesktop&amp;hl=en-GB">Chrome</a></li>
<li><a href="https://support.mozilla.org/en-US/kb/clear-cookies-and-site-data-firefox">Firefox</a></li>
<li><a href="https://support.microsoft.com/en-us/microsoft-edge/delete-cookies-in-microsoft-edge-63947406-40ac-c3b8-57b9-2a946a29ae09">Edge</a></li>
<li><a href="https://support.apple.com/guide/safari/manage-cookies-and-website-data-sfri11471/mac">Safari</a></li>
</ul>
<p>Note: Refusing or deleting cookies only affects the Device and the browser on which you perform this action. If you use different Devices and/or browsers you will need to repeat the above described actions on these Devices and/or browsers.</p>
<h2 id="privacy">Privacy</h2>
<p>It is possible that information collected through a cookie or obtained otherwise, contains personal data. If this is the case, our Privacy Policy is applicable on the processing of these data. The Privacy Policy can be read <a href="/legal/privacy-policy/">here</a>.</p>
<h2 id="can-this-cookie-policy-be-changed">Can this Cookie Policy be changed?</h2>
<p>We may amend this Cookie Policy in the future. If there are substantive or material changes that may affect one or more of the parties involved to a considerable extent, we inform those involved in advance. Our changed Cookie Policy will also be available on this web page, so it is recommended to regularly have a look at this page.</p>
<h2 id="overview-cookies">Overview cookies</h2>
